## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="24ab3-1356">Windows Server 2012 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24ab3-1356">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24ab3-1357">此類別包含 Windows Server 2012 的下列屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24ab3-1357">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="24ab3-1787">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24ab3-1787">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24ab3-1788">**MS DFSR 訂** 用帳戶類別是分散式檔案系統 (DFS) Replication service 支援的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24ab3-1788">The **ms-DFSR-Subscription** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
